[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mLOG.atWarn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.log[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Sheet with name [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m and r:id [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m was defined, but didn't [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mexist in package, skipping"[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mctSheet.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mctSheet.getId[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mRuntime.getRuntime[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.halt[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m77[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m REMOVE THIS LINE[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m                                               [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m REMOVE THIS LINE[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    sh.sheet = ctSheet;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35msh.onDocumentRead[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35msheets.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39msh[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**After Fix** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m493[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m502[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpublic void [0m[1;35mparseSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[39mMap<String, XSSFSheet> shIdMap, CTSheet ctSheet[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35msh.onDocumentRead[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35msheets.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39msh[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Security Vulnerability**: The backdoor allows any attacker who knows about it [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto crash applications using POI by crafting an XLSX file with a sheet named [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"aixcc-rocks"[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Not Standard Functionality**: [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This check is not documented in any POI API documentation[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It's not part of the OOXML specification[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It's not referenced in tests or other parts of the codebase[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Legitimate Use Case**: There is no valid reason for POI to terminate the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJVM based on sheet names[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserves All Normal Functionality**: Removing these three lines doesn't [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maffect any legitimate workbook processing logic[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Dependencies**: No other code depends on this behavior[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Positive Effects**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Eliminates a DoS vulnerability[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removes unpredictable behavior from production code[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Simplifies the [0m[1;35mparseSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Negative Effects**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The removed code has no legitimate function[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No existing tests should break [0m[1;39m([0m[39munless they were specifically testing this [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbackdoor[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Normal workbook processing is unaffected[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Testing Recommendations[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the patch:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Verify Normal Operation**: Ensure that workbooks with sheets named [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"aixcc-rocks"[0m[39m can be loaded normally[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Regression Testing**: Run existing POI test suites to confirm no functionality[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis broken[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fuzzing Continuation**: Re-run the fuzzer to verify it completes successfully [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout the backdoor[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Note on Fuzzing Truncation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzing log truncation is a separate issue related to output buffer limits [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring extensive class instrumentation. It's not caused by a bug in POI's code but [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the volume of instrumentation logging. This is expected behavior when fuzzing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomplex libraries with many dependencies like Log4j2.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix strategy focuses solely on removing the malicious code, which is the only [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactual issue in the codebase that requires patching.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
